<script>
function add_byoc_level(level, id) {
if (typeof BYOC_LEVELS[level] == 'undefined') {
BYOC_LEVELS[level] = new Array();
}
// Make sure we don't accidentally end up with the same id twice!
for (var i=0; i < BYOC_LEVELS[level].length; i++) {
if (BYOC_LEVELS[level][i] == id) {
return;
}
}
BYOC_LEVELS[level].push(id);
}
</script>
